# cd /Users/jesse/Documents/GitHub/keyboardio/firmware/Keyboardio-Factory-Programming/Model-100/firmware-builder/repos/attiny_bootloader/TWI_Slave
# make all
avr-gcc -fverbose-asm -g -Wall -Wextra -Werror -pedantic -Os -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000  -Wl,--section-start=.text=0x1C00 -c twi_slave.c -o twi_slave.o
avr-gcc -fverbose-asm -g -Wall -Wextra -Werror -pedantic -Os -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000  -Wl,--section-start=.text=0x1C00 -o twi_slave.elf twi_slave.o
rm -f twi_slave.hex
avr-objcopy -j .text -j .data -O ihex twi_slave.elf twi_slave.hex
avr-size --format=avr --mcu=attiny88 twi_slave.elf
AVR Memory Usage
----------------
Device: attiny88

Program:     882 bytes (10.8% Full)
(.text + .data + .bootloader)

Data:         66 bytes (12.9% Full)
(.data + .bss + .noinit)


# write bootloader jump vector to beginning
sed -i'' -e '$ d' twi_slave.hex # two dollar signs because Make otherwise interprets them
# write a new vector table to jump to the bootloader
# rjmp to 0x1C00, etc.
echo ':02000000FFCD32' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02000200FFCD30' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02000400FFCD2E' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02000600FFCD2C' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02000800FFCD2A' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02000A00FFCD28' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02000C00FFCD26' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02000E00FFCD24' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02001000FFCD22' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02001200FFCD20' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02001400FFCD1E' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02001600FFCD1C' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02001800FFCD1A' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02001A00FFCD18' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02001C00FFCD16' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02001E00FFCD14' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02002000FFCD12' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02002200FFCD10' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02002400FFCD0E' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02002600FFCD0C' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':02002800FFCD0A' >> twi_slave.hex
echo ':00000001FF' >> twi_slave.hex

make -C firmware PRODUCT_ID=keyboardio-model-100
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -c main.c -o main.o
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -c twi-slave.c -o twi-slave.o
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -c ringbuf.c -o ringbuf.o
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -c wire-protocol.c -o wire-protocol.o
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -c keyscanner.c -o keyscanner.o
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -c led-apa102c.c -o led-apa102c.o
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -c led-issi31fl3743b.c -o led-issi31fl3743b.o
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -c led-ws2812b.c -o led-ws2812b.o
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -c led-null.c -o led-null.o
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -x assembler-with-cpp -c nops.S -o nops.o
avr-gcc -Wall -Wextra -O3 -std=gnu11 -flto -mmcu=attiny88 -DF_CPU=8000000 -include "config/keyboardio-model-100.h" -fverbose-asm -g -funroll-loops -o main.elf main.o twi-slave.o ringbuf.o wire-protocol.o keyscanner.o led-apa102c.o led-issi31fl3743b.o led-ws2812b.o led-null.o nops.o
rm -f main.hex

avr-size --format=avr --mcu=attiny88 main.elf

mkdir -p out/dist
